Summary:
Added types to (almost) all untyped instances of NSArray and NSMutableArray.

```
Added types to 103 instances of NSArray and NSMutableArray (107 - 4)

Before:
ack --ignore-dir samples &#39;(NSMutableArray|NSArray) \*&#39; -hc
107

After:
ack --ignore-dir samples &#39;(NSMutableArray|NSArray) \*&#39; -hc
4

Out of those added 26 (36 - 13) used &lt;id&gt; if a more specific type could not be added

Before:
ack --ignore-dir samples &#39;(NSMutableArray|NSArray)&lt;id&gt; \*&#39; -hc
13

After:
ack --ignore-dir samples &#39;(NSMutableArray|NSArray)&lt;id&gt; \*&#39; -hc
36
```

                    <a data-pjax="true" title="Add a swiftlint rule to prefer final classes

Summary:
There were only 2 instances in which I had to add a disable comment for prefer_final_classes due to subclassing

Used the following to add the final keyword (Adds final to any class that doesn&#39;t have final or open before it and doesn&#39;t have func after it)
```
find . -name &#39;*.swift&#39; | xargs perl -pi -e &#39;s/(?&lt;!final )(?&lt;!open )(class (?!func).*\{)/final \1/g&#39;
```

          <div role="gridcell" class="flex-auto min-width-0 d-none d-md-block col-5 mr-3" >
              <span class="css-truncate css-truncate-target d-block width-fit markdown-title">
                    <a data-pjax="true" title="Remove the line from .gitattributes that treats pbxproj files as binary (#1561)

Summary:
Pull Request resolved: https://github.com/facebook/facebook-ios-sdk/pull/1561

The &quot;*.pbxproj binary merge=union&quot; line was added in a prior commit (D18655686 (https://github.com/facebook/facebook-ios-sdk/commit/c54b37a25c5b407959b6c087931bb8c34bb1c163)) as a way to automatically resolve merge conflicts in Xcode project files based on this article: https://thoughtbot.com/blog/xcode-and-git-bridging-the-gap

The article doesn&#39;t specify why the pbxproj file should be treated as a binary, however one side effect is that the `git diff` command will no longer show changes in the project file.

For example if a project file is changed it will just show the following:
```
Binary files a/FBSDKGamingServicesKit/FBSDKGamingServicesKit.xcodeproj/project.pbxproj and b/FBSDKGamingServicesKit/FBSDKGamingServicesKit.xcodeproj/project.pbxproj differ
```

It doesn&#39;t seem like the binary attribute is necessary to use the merge=union strategy as the following article
https://roadfiresoftware.com/2015/09/automatically-resolving-git-merge-conflicts-in-xcodes-project-pbxproj/

However I&#39;m not convinced that we need the merge=union strategy since resolving conflicts in project files is fairly simple and mostly only occurs when two files have been added in the same location in the project. Even then the conflict is easy to resolve.

Furthermore it doesn&#39;t look like this strategy works reliably. This StackOverflow answer indicates that the user tried this strategy and ended up removing it since it didn&#39;t work in about 1 of 4 cases: https://stackoverflow.com/a/18275082. (When it doesn&#39;t work it will prevent the project from being opened at all and would have to fixed manually anyway).

And finally, if there is a conflict between two similarly named files that have been added to the location in the project file, resolving the conflict manually allows the alphabetical order of the files to be corrected if needed.

Reviewed By: joesus

          <div role="gridcell" class="flex-auto min-width-0 d-none d-md-block col-5 mr-3" >
              <span class="css-truncate css-truncate-target d-block width-fit markdown-title">
                    <a data-pjax="true" title="Complete restructuring/renaming of FacebookGamingServices to FBSDKGamingServicesKit

Summary:
Context:
We currently have 2 gaming modules FacebookGamingServices and FBSDKGamingServicesKit

FacebookGamingServices is currently the main module and FBSDKGamingServicesKit is a wrapper around it. The FBSDKGamingServicesKit wrapper previously included 2 Objective-C wrappers to expose functionality in Swift-only code in FacebookGamingServices. However, the maintenance cost of maintaining 2 separate modules was very high so these are being combined into one module.

For this, all of the Objective-C wrappers have been moved to FacebookGamingServices so FBSDKGamingServicesKit is now just an empty wrapper around FacebookGamingServices.

In this diff, I&#39;ve made the FBSDKGamingServicesKit module the main module and made FacebookGamingServices be a wrapper around it, as we are doing for other kits for Swift Package Manager.

Reviewed By: samodom

          <div role="gridcell" class="flex-auto min-width-0 d-none d-md-block col-5 mr-3" >
              <span class="css-truncate css-truncate-target d-block width-fit markdown-title">
                    <a data-pjax="true" title="Complete restructuring/renaming of FacebookGamingServices to FBSDKGamingServicesKit

Summary:
Context:
We currently have 2 gaming modules FacebookGamingServices and FBSDKGamingServicesKit

FacebookGamingServices is currently the main module and FBSDKGamingServicesKit is a wrapper around it. The FBSDKGamingServicesKit wrapper previously included 2 Objective-C wrappers to expose functionality in Swift-only code in FacebookGamingServices. However, the maintenance cost of maintaining 2 separate modules was very high so these are being combined into one module.

For this, all of the Objective-C wrappers have been moved to FacebookGamingServices so FBSDKGamingServicesKit is now just an empty wrapper around FacebookGamingServices.

In this diff, I&#39;ve made the FBSDKGamingServicesKit module the main module and made FacebookGamingServices be a wrapper around it, as we are doing for other kits for Swift Package Manager.

Reviewed By: samodom

          <h2 class="Box-title">
            <a href="#readme" data-view-component="true" class="Link--primary">README.md</a>
          </h2>
        </div>
      </div>

        <div data-target="readme-toc.content" class="Box-body px-5 pb-5">
          <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-facebook-sdk-for-ios" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#facebook-sdk-for-ios"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Facebook SDK for iOS</h1>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://cocoapods.org/pods/FBSDKCoreKit" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/d1f5c6fb5cfedfd1b1d4cee579d45dddbbf7c2adaeac967794b10dc29a87e419/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f636f636f61706f64732f702f464253444b436f72654b69742e737667" alt="Platforms" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/cocoapods/p/FBSDKCoreKit.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://circleci.com/gh/facebook/facebook-ios-sdk/tree/main" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/535f8bb856e05b22046cc62a3878cbbb568adfa0ccd69054cc2dce50f0db0530/68747470733a2f2f636972636c6563692e636f6d2f67682f66616365626f6f6b2f66616365626f6f6b2d696f732d73646b2f747265652f6d61696e2e7376673f7374796c653d736869656c64" alt="circleci" data-canonical-src="https://circleci.com/gh/facebook/facebook-ios-sdk/tree/main.svg?style=shield" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://cocoapods.org/pods/FBSDKCoreKit" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/5dfc8a8975123f0ffd21516081d3168988769ac89efdffaba7ea299a833fb838/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f636f636f61706f64732f762f464253444b436f72654b69742e737667" alt="CocoaPods" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/cocoapods/v/FBSDKCoreKit.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c8961b92aa4c1cece705532f044860ab81846426578305a5e8d83c0f357de8c2/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f43617274686167652d636f6d70617469626c652d3442433531442e7376673f7374796c653d666c6174" alt="Carthage compatible" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Carthage-compatible-4BC51D.svg?style=flat" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">This open-source library allows you to integrate Facebook into your iOS app.</p>
<p dir="auto">Learn more about the provided samples, documentation, integrating the SDK into your app, accessing source code, and more
at <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/docs/ios" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/docs/ios</a></p>
<p dir="auto">Please take a moment and <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/enterprise/2.15/user/articles/watching-and-unwatching-repositories">subscribe to releases</a> so that you can be notified about new features, deprecations, and critical fixes. To see information about the latest release, consult our <a href="/facebook/facebook-ios-sdk/blob/main/CHANGELOG.md">changelog</a>.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/26a0.png"></g-emoji> Be Advised <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/26a0.png"></g-emoji></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left"><p dir="auto">We have begun rewriting the iOS SDK in Swift in order to modernize the code base.</p><p dir="auto">Please monitor the changelog for updates to existing interfaces but keep in mind that some interfaces will be unstable during this process. As such, updating to a minor version may introduce compilation issues related to language interoperability.</p>Please bear with us as we work towards providing an improved experience for integrating with the Facebook platform.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-try-it-out" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#try-it-out"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>TRY IT OUT</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-swift-package-manager" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#swift-package-manager"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Swift Package Manager</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>In Xcode, select File &gt; Swift Packages &gt; Add Package Dependency.</li>
<li>Follow the prompts using the URL for this repository</li>
<li>Select the <code>Facebook</code>-prefixed libraries you want to use</li>
<li>Check-out the tutorials available online at: <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/docs/ios/getting-started" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/docs/ios/getting-started</a></li>
<li>Start coding! Visit <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/docs/ios" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/docs/ios</a> for tutorials and reference documentation.</li>
</ol>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-ios-14-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ios-14-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>iOS 14 CHANGES</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-data-disclosure" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#data-disclosure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Data Disclosure</h3>
<p dir="auto">Due to the release of iOS 14, tracking events that your app collects and sends to Facebook may require you to disclosed these data types in the App Store Connect questionnaire. It is your responsibility to ensure this is reflected in your applications privacy policy. Visit our blogpost for information on affected Facebook SDKs, APIs, and products and the Apple App Store Privacy Details article to learn more about the data types you will need to disclose.</p>
<p dir="auto">link to FB blogpost <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/blog/post/2020/10/22/preparing-for-apple-app-store-data-disclosure-requirements/" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/blog/post/2020/10/22/preparing-for-apple-app-store-data-disclosure-requirements/</a></p>
<p dir="auto">apple store details <a href="https://developer.apple.com/app-store/app-privacy-details/" rel="nofollow">https://developer.apple.com/app-store/app-privacy-details/</a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-features" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>FEATURES</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Login - <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/docs/facebook-login" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/docs/facebook-login</a></li>
<li>Sharing - <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/docs/sharing" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/docs/sharing</a></li>
<li>App Links - <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/docs/applinks" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/docs/applinks</a></li>
<li>Graph API - <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/docs/ios/graph" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/docs/ios/graph</a></li>
<li>Analytics - <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/docs/analytics" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/docs/analytics</a></li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-give-feedback" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#give-feedback"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>GIVE FEEDBACK</h2>
<p dir="auto">Please report bugs or issues to our designated developer support team -- <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/support/bugs/" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/support/bugs/</a> -- as this will help us resolve them more quickly.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can also visit our <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/community/" rel="nofollow">Facebook Developer Community Forum</a>,
join the <a href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/fbdevelopers/" rel="nofollow">Facebook Developers Group on Facebook</a>,
ask questions on <a href="http://facebook.stackoverflow.com" rel="nofollow">Stack Overflow</a>,
or open an issue in this repository.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-contribute" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#contribute"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>CONTRIBUTE</h2>
<p dir="auto">Facebook welcomes contributions to our SDKs. Please see the <a href="/facebook/facebook-ios-sdk/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md">CONTRIBUTING</a> file.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-license" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#license"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>LICENSE</h2>
<p dir="auto">See the <a href="/facebook/facebook-ios-sdk/blob/main/LICENSE">LICENSE</a> file.</p>
<p dir="auto">Copyright  Meta Platforms, Inc</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-security-policy" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#security-policy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>SECURITY POLICY</h2>
<p dir="auto">See the <a href="/facebook/facebook-ios-sdk/blob/main/SECURITY.md">SECURITY POLICY</a> for more info on our bug bounty program.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-developer-terms" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#developer-terms"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DEVELOPER TERMS</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>By enabling Facebook integrations, including through this SDK, you can share information with Facebook, including
information about peoples use of your app. Facebook will use information received in accordance with our
<a href="https://www.facebook.com/about/privacy/" rel="nofollow">Data Use Policy</a>, including to provide you with insights about the
effectiveness of your ads and the use of your app. These integrations also enable us and our partners to serve ads on
and off Facebook.</li>
<li>You may limit your sharing of information with us by updating the Insights control in the developer tool
<code>https://developers.facebook.com/apps/{app_id}/settings/advanced</code>.</li>
<li>If you use a Facebook integration, including to share information with us, you agree and confirm that you have
provided appropriate and sufficiently prominent notice to and obtained the appropriate consent from your users
regarding such collection, use, and disclosure (including, at a minimum, through your privacy policy). You further
agree that you will not share information with us about children under the age of 13.</li>
<li>You agree to comply with all applicable laws and regulations and also agree to our Terms
<a href="https://www.facebook.com/policies/" rel="nofollow">https://www.facebook.com/policies/</a>, including our Platform Policies <a href="https://developers.facebook.com/policy/" rel="nofollow">https://developers.facebook.com/policy/</a> and
Advertising Guidelines, as applicable <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ad_guidelines.php" rel="nofollow">https://www.facebook.com/ad_guidelines.php</a>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">By using the Facebook SDK for iOS you agree to these terms.</p>
</article>
